total</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> revenue</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, a decrease of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">about </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">10</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> basis points</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">compared to the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">second</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">quarter of 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><a name="_Hlk109026257"></a><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">This decrease results</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> from</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">the benefit of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">menu price increases</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> taken in the prior year</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">and lower avocado prices, which w</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">ere</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> partially</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> offset by</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">inflation across several food costs, primarily </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">beef, tortillas, dairy, salsa, beans and rice</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">Restaurant level operating margin </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">in the second quarter </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">was 2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">7.5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">compared to</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">5.2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">% in the </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">second</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> quarter of 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">. The </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">improvement</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> was</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> primarily </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">due to </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">the benefit of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">sales leverage</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> and, to a lesser extent, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">lower avocado prices</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> These decreases were partially offset by higher </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">inflation across several food cost</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">s</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">, &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">and to a lesser extent, wage inflation</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">.</font>
		</p>

		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Average restaurant sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">refer to the average trailing 12-month food and beverage revenue for restaurants in operation for at least 12 full calendar months.</font><a name="_Hlk74719682"></a></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Restaurant level operating margin</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">represents total revenue less direct restaurant operating costs, expressed as a percent of total revenue.</font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
				<font style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Symbol;border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9;color:#000000;font-size:10pt;;"> &#xB7;</font>
			</p>
		</td><td style="width:0pt;"><p style="width:0pt;width:0pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td align="left" valign="top">
			<p style="border-top:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;border-bottom:1pt none #D9D9D9 ;color:#000000;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt;margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">Digital sales</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;"> represent food and beverage revenue generated through the Chipotle website, Chipotle app or third-party delivery aggregators. Digital sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">include revenue deferrals associated with Chipotle Rewards. </font></p></td></tr></table></div>
		<div style="width:100%"><table style="width:100%; table-layout: fixed;" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0"><tr><td style="width:18pt;"><p style="width:18pt;font-size:0pt;"></p></td><td valign="top" align="left" style="width: 18.00pt;">

			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">In-restaurant sales </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;color:#000000;">represent food and beverage revenue generated on-premise. In-restaurant sales includes revenue deferrals associated with Chipotle Rewards. </font></p></td></tr></table></div></div><div style="margin-left:36pt;margin-right:36pt;">

		<p style="margin:13.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-weight:bold;color:#000000;">About Chipotle</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 0pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Chipotle Mexican Grill, Inc. (NYSE: CMG) is cultivating a better world by serving responsibly sourced, classically-cooked, real food with wholesome ingredients without artificial colors, flavors or preservatives. Chipotle had </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">over</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">3,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">2</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">5</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> restaurants as of </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">June 30</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">, 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">, in the United States, Canada, the United Kingdom, France and Germany and is the only restaurant company of its size that owns and operates all its restaurants</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> in North America and Europe</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">. &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">Chipotle is ranked on the Fortune 500 and is recognized on the 202</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">3</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> list for Fortune&#x2019;s Most Admired Companies</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;"> and Time Magazine&#x2019;s Most Influential Companies</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">. &nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">With </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">over</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">&nbsp;</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">1</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">0</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">,000 em</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">ployees passionate about providing a great guest experience, Chipotle is a longtime leader and innovator in the fo</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;">od industry. Chipotle is committed to making its food more accessible to everyone while continuing to be a brand with a demonstrated purpose as it leads the way in digital, technology and sustainable business practices. For more information or to place an order online, visit </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;text-transform:uppercase;color:#C08C19;background-color: #FFFFFF;">WWW.CHIPOTLE.COM</font><font style="display: inline;">.</font>

These statements are subject to risks and uncertainties that could cause actual results to differ materially from those described in the statements, including but not limited to: increasing wage inflation and the competitive labor market, which impacts our ability to attract and retain qualified employees and has resulted in occasional staffing shortages; the impact of any union organizing efforts and our responses to such efforts; increasing supply costs (including beef, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">tortillas, dairy</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> salsa, beans and rice</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">); the impact of competition, including from sources outside the restaurant industry; the financial impact of increasing our average hourly wages; the impact of federal, state or local government regulations relating to our employees, employment practices, restaurant design and construction, and the sale of food or alcoholic beverages; our ability to achieve our planned growth, such as the availability of suitable new restaurant sites and the availability of construction materials and contractors; increases in ingredient and other operating costs due </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">to inflation, global conflicts, climate change, </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">our Food </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">w</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">ith Integrity philosophy, tariffs or trade restrictions and supply shortages; the uncertainty of our ability to achieve expected levels of comparable restaurant sales due to factors such as changes in consumers' perceptions of our brand, including as a result of actual or rumored food safety concerns or other negative publicity, decreased consumer spending (including as a result of higher inflation, mass layoffs, fear of possible recession and higher energy prices), or the inability to increase menu prices or realize the benefits of menu price increases; risks associated with our digital business, including risks arising from our reliance on third party delivery services; risks relating to litigation, including possible governmental actions </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">and potentially class action litigation </font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">related to food safety incidents</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;">, cybersecurity incidents,</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> employment</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> or privacy</font><font style="display: inline;font-family:Calibri;font-style:italic;"> laws, advertising claims or other matters; 		<p style="margin:0pt 0pt 3pt;text-align:center;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;font-weight:bold;">RECONCILIATION OF NON-GAAP FINANCIAL MEASURES</font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:13pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<a name="_Hlk22568764"></a><font style="display: inline;">The following tables provide a reconciliation of non-GAAP financial measures presented in the text above to the most directly comparable financial measures calculated and presented in accordance with GAAP. </font>
		</p>
		<p style="margin:4.5pt 0pt 9pt;font-family:Times New Roman;font-size: 10pt">
			<font style="display: inline;">Adjusted net income is net income excluding expenses related to </font><font style="display: inline;color:#000000;">restaurant and corporate asset impairment, corporate restructuring, certain legal proceedings, stock-</font><font style="display: inline;">based compensation modification expense, unrealized gains on equity investments, separation costs, and certain other costs. Adjusted general and administrative expense is general and administrative expense excluding corporate restructuring, certain legal proceedings, stock-based compensation modification expense, separation costs, and certain other costs. The adjusted effective income tax rate is the effective income tax rate adjusted to reflect the after tax impact of non-GAAP adjustments. Restaurant Level Operating Margin, a non-GAAP financial measure, is equal to the revenues generated by our restaurants less their direct operating costs which consist of food, beverage and packaging, labor, occupancy and other operating costs. This performance measure primarily includes the costs that restaurant level managers can directly control and excludes other costs that are essential to conduct our business. Management uses restaurant level operating margin as a measure of restaurant performance. Management believes restaurant level operating margin is useful to investors in that it highlights trends in our core business that may not otherwise be apparent to investors when relying solely on GAAP financial measures. We present these non-GAAP measures in order to facilitate meaningful evaluation of our operating performance across periods. These adjustments are intended to provide greater transparency of underlying performance and to allow investors to evaluate our business on the same basis as our management, which uses these non-GAAP measures in evaluating the company&#x2019;s performance. Our adjusted net income, adjusted diluted earnings per share, adjusted general and administrative expenses, adjusted effective income tax rate and restaurant level operating margin measures may not be comparable to other companies&#x2019; adjusted measures. These adjustments are not necessarily indicative of what our actual financial performance would have been during the periods presented and should be viewed in addition to, and not as an alternative to, our results prepared in accordance with GAAP. Further details regarding these adjustments are included in the tables below.</font>
		</p>

var Show={};Show.LastAR=null,Show.showAR=function(a,r,w){if(Show.LastAR)Show.hideAR();var e=a;while(e&&e.nodeName!='TABLE')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e||e.nodeName!='TABLE'){var ref=((window)?w.document:document).getElementById(r);if(ref){e=ref.cloneNode(!0);
e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
e.style.display=d;if(a.textContent){a.textContent=p+a.textContent.substring(1)}else{a.innerText=p+a.innerText.substring(1)}}}
